    Moa Moa No Mi (Increasing Quality)

    Devil Fruit, Rare

    Type. Environment Alterer Paramecia

    Fruit appearance. This fruit resembles a gleaming, oversized pearl with shimmering hues of blue and silver. Its surface pulses with a soft light, and has a swirling, thick stem.

    Description. The Moa Moa No Mi grants its user the incredible ability to amplify the inherent qualities of any object or creature they touch, making them larger, faster, and more potent.

    Sea Weakness. You are weak to water and seastone.

    Qualitative Touch. You learn the Magic Stone cantrip. As an action, you can touch an object or creature. Depending on your intent, you can magnify one of the following qualities:

    • Size: You can increase the size of the touched object or creature by one category (up to gargantuan). If a creature is enlarged in this manner, it gains the benefits of the Enlarge/Reduce spell (only enlarge). This increase lasts for 1 minute.

    • Speed: You double the movement speed of the touched object or creature for 1 round.

    • Strength: You amplify the strength of the touched object or creature. If an object is enhanced, its damage threshold increases by 20. If a creature is enhanced in this manner, it gains advantage on Strength checks, Strength Saves, and Strength-based attack rolls. This boost lasts for 1 round.

    Empowerment Pulse. As an action, you can expend 1 devil fruit charge to release a wave of energy in a 30-foot radius. All allies within this radius have one of the qualities (Size, Speed, or Strength) enhanced, as per your Qualitative Touch, until the end of your next turn.

    Spells (Amplification Techniques). This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Catapult (1 charge, and can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), Jump (1 charge), Enhance Ability (2 charges), Conjure Barrage (3 charges), Haste (3 charges), Freedom of Movement (4 charges), Conjure Volley (5 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

    Awakening (Qualitative Realm). Once you've awakened your power, as an action you can envelop a 30-foot radius around you in a shimmering dome for 1 minute or until you fall unconscious. Within this realm, the very air seems charged with energy. All objects and allies inside gain all the benefits of your Qualitative Touch simultaneously, while enemies find one of their qualities diminished if they fail a Constitution saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC when the dome is created (Size is reduced by one category, Speed is halved, or Strength-based attacks deal 1d4 less damage) for the duration. A creature which has its equalities diminished can repeat the saving throw at the end of each of its turns. Once you activate this awakening, you can't do so again for another 24 hours.

    Buki Buki No Mi (Armory)

    Devil Fruit, Rare

    Type. Body Enhancer Paramecia

    Fruit appearance. The Buki Buki no Mi looks akin to a steel-gray pomegranate with sharp, angular facets. Its sheen reflects light as if made of polished metal, and the stem is shaped like the handle of a small dagger.

    Description. The Buki Buki No Mi allows its user to transform parts of their body, or even their entire form, into various weapons. This unique power renders the user a veritable one-person armory, aptly termed a Full-Body Weapon Human.

    Sea Weakness. You are weak to water and seastone.

    Weapon Morphing. As a bonus action, you can transform a part of your body into any weapon (e.g., swords, shields, bows, firearms, etc.), it's considered magical for the purpose of overcoming resistance. You can use this part of your body as a weapon attack, and you are proficient with it. You can only use one weapon active this way at a time, and can dismiss it using a bonus action.

    Full-Body Arsenal. As an action, you can morph your entire body into a larger weapon or siege equipment (like a ballista or catapult). While in this form, you cannot move or take other actions, but allies can use the weaponized form to attack. This transformation lasts for 1 minute or until you end it as a bonus action.

    Impenetrable Defense. Your AC can’t be less than 18, regardless of what kind of armor you are wearing. By spending 1 devil fruit charge as a bonus action, you can gain a +2 bonus to your AC for up to 1 minute or until you fall unconscious (this effect doesn't stack).

    Spells (Weapon Techniques). This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Thunderous Smite (1 charge), Cloud of Daggers (2 charges, and can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), Conjure Barrage (3 charges), Staggering Smite (4 charges), Stoneskin (Self; 4 charges), Conjure Volley (5 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

    Awakening (Living Armory). Once you've awakened your power, as an action, you create a whirlwind of shifting weaponry around you for 1 minute or until you fall unconscious. Blades, firearms, and other armaments constantly morph and reshape across your body. For the next minute, whenever a creature starts its turn within 30 feet of you or moves into that area for the first time on a turn it must make a Dexterity saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC. On a failure, it takes 6d10 bludgeoning, piercing or, slashing damage from the weapons, or half as much on a success. After using this feature, you cannot use it again for another 24 hours.

    Pamu Pamu No Mi (Rupture)

    Devil Fruit, Rare

    Type. Environment Alterer Paramecia

    Fruit appearance. The Pamu Pamu no Mi is a vivid crimson fruit with a rough, bumpy surface reminiscent of eruptive textures.

    Description. The Pamu Pamu No Mi grants its user the ability to make any object they touch swell and erupt on command. The eruption's strength can vary, from a simple pop to a massive blast.

    Sea Weakness. You are weak to water and seastone.

    Explosion Immunity You gain immunity to thunder damage.

    Touch of Detonation. As an action, you can touch an inanimate object or part of a surface, imbuing no larger than a 5-foot area of it with eruptive energy. As a bonus action on subsequent turns, you can detonate the object if it is within 60-feet of you, causing it to erupt and explode and deal 3d8 thunder damage to all creatures within a 10-foot radius of the touched spot. The explosion destroys the object if it is medium-size, and destroys a 5-foot cube of the surface if it is nonmagical. Only a number of spots equal to your proficiency bonus can remain imbued by this ability at a time, and it can only remain explosive in this way for 1 hour.

The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

    Awakening (Omnipresent Detonation). Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to cast Reality Break, without expending a spell slot or material components, as you cause space and time around the target to rupture randomly. You can't use this action again for another 24 hours.

    Wapu Wapu No Mi (Teleporting)

    Devil Fruit, Rare

    Type. Environment Alterer Paramecia

    Description. The Wapu Wapu No Mi gives its user the remarkable ability to teleport themselves and, to a limited extent, other objects or people. With a thought, the user can vanish from one location and reappear in another.

    Sea Weakness. You are weak to water and seastone.

    Blinking Step. As a bonus action, you can teleport to any location you can see within 60 feet. You must have a clear line of sight to your destination.

    Fude Fude No Mi (Paintbrush)

    Devil Fruit, Rare

    Type. Environment Alterer Paramecia

    Fruit appearance. The Fude Fude no Mi is a gradient fruit, transitioning from dark indigo at its top to a pastel pink at its base. It feels like soft bristles to the touch, with swirled patterns reminiscent of flowing ink or paint.

    Description. The Fude Fude No Mi grants its user the mystical ability to bring their artistic creations to life. By drawing or painting with their hands or tools, the user can create tangible, functioning objects or creatures from their imagination.

    Sea Weakness. You are weak to water and seastone.

    Artist's Knowledge. You can spend an action to manifest Painter's supplies into your hands, which you are proficient with. You have advantage on any check made using Painter's Supplies.

    Artistic Creation. As an action, you can spend 1 devil fruit charge to paint a creature or an object on a surface, then peel it off to make it manifest for up to 1 hour. You must maintain concentration on this power to keep it (like concentration on a spell), or else the creature will return to your book. This can create simple objects no larger than huge or non-hostile, non-magical beasts (like horses, dogs, etc.) with a CR no greater than 1. The created creatures are friendly to you and your companions and follow simple commands.

    Spells (Artistic Techniques). This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Ink Cloud (Fog Cloud; 1 charge, and can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), Find Steed (2 charges), Conjure Animals (3 charges), Conjure Barrage (3 charges), Conjure Woodland Beings (4 charges), Conjure Minor Elemetnals (4 charges), Find Greater Steed (4 charges), Conjure Elemental (5 charges), Conjure Volley (5 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

    Awakening (Final Masterpiece). Once you've awakened your power, as an action, you can cast Animal Shapes, without expending a spell slot or material components. Instead of targeting creatures, you instead target a number of animal artpieces you've created on a surface within range to transform. After using this feature, you cannot use it again for another 24 hours.

    CHAPTER 2 | RARE PARAMECIA

    \page

    Ito Ito No Mi (String)

    Devil Fruit, Rare

    Type. Substance Generator Paramecia

    Fruit appearance. The Ito Ito no Mi is a light gray pear with swirling patterns on its surface.

    Description. This coveted Devil Fruit allows its user to create, manipulate, and control string. The user's mastery over string can be employed for both offensive and defensive purposes, as well as for puppetry, ensnaring, or even flight.

    Sea Weakness. You are weak to water and seastone.

    String Creation. As a bonus action, you can create strings from any part of your body, which last for 1 minute. These strings are incredibly durable and sharp, and extend up to 120 feet from you. You can make a ranged weapon attack with them, dealing 2d8 slashing damage on a hit. You are proficient with these strings, and you can use Dexterity or Strength for the attack and damage rolls.

    Additionally, you can use an action to attempt to trap a creature you can see within 120 feet in your strings. The creature must make a Strength saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC or become restrained by string.

    A creature restrained by the string can use its action to make a Strength check against your Devil Fruit save DC. If it succeeds, it is no longer restrained.

    String Puppetry. As an action, you can attempt to control a creautre you have restrained with your strings. The creature must succeed on a Strength saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC or be controlled by you until the start of your next turn. While controlled, the creature moves and acts as you dictate on its turn.

    Bird Cage. As an action, you can spend 6 devil fruit charges to cast Wall of Force, no material components required. However, you can only form it into a hemispherical dome with a radius of 10 miles. While you maintain concentration on this wall, you can use an action to decrease its radius by 1 mile once per minute. The decrease doesn't happen immediately, but rather slowly over the next minute. Nonmagical objects are pushed along with the wall when the radius decreases, or get destroyed if they are fixed in place. The wall does not extend into the material plane.

    Spells (String Techniques). This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: String Tentacles (Arms of Hadar, but deals bludgeoning damage; 1 charge, and can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), Web (2 charges), Hold Person (2 charges, and can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), String Puppet (Crown of Madness; 2 charges), String Clones (Mirror Image; 2 charges), Sky Path (Fly; 3 charges), String Parade (Compulsion; 4 charges), or Hold Monster (5 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

    Awakening (String World). Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to cast Blade Barrier, without expending spell slots or material components, by creating sharp string sheets from objects around you. While the Blade Barrier is active, you can use a bonus action on your turn to move and reshape the blades in any way you choose (up to the range of the spell).

    Additionally, as an action, you can sacrifice up to 10 feet of the blade barrier in diameter and length to use God Thread. When you do so, you shoot out a sharp arrow of concentrated string a 100 foot long and 5 foot line originating from you. Any creature in the line must make a Dexterity save against your Devil Fruit save DC. A creature takes 6d10 piercing damage on a failed save, or half as much damage on a successful one.

    After using this feature, you cannot use it again for another 24 hours.

    CHAPTER 2 | RARE PARAMECIA

    \page

    Haipa Haipa No Mi (Super Speed)

    Devil Fruit, Rare

    Type. Body Enhancer Paramecia

    Fruit appearance. The Haipa Haipa No Mi is a pineapple with a shimmering silver-blue hue. It has patterns that resemble trails of gusty winds wrapping around it.

    Description. The Haipa Haipa No Mi bestows its user with unparalleled speed, reflexes, and the ability to think at an accelerated rate, making them a true "Speed Human".

    Sea Weakness. You are weak to water and seastone.

    Unparalleled speed. You gain a +30 feet bonus to your movement speed.

    Quick Reflexes. You can spend 1 devil fruit charge as a bonus action to take the dodge, disengage, or dash action.

    Evasion. Your instinctive agility lets you dodge out of the way of certain area effects, such as a blue dragon's lightning breath or a fireball spell. When you are subjected to an effect that allows you to make a Dexterity saving throw to take only half damage, you instead take no damage if you succeed on the saving throw, and only half damage if you fail.

    Spells (Velocity Techniques). This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Jump (Self; 1 charge), Blur (2 charges), Misty Step (2 charges), Haste (Self; 3 charges), Freedom of Movement (Self; 4 charges), Steel Wind Strike (5 charges), Swift Quiver (5 charges), or Far Step (5 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

    Awakening (Mass Acceleration). Once you've awakened your power, as an action, you can create a zone of accelerated time in a 120-foot radius centered on yourself. Inside this zone, all allies' speed is doubled, and they gain advantage on Dexterity saving throws. Any hostile creature's speed is halved, and they have disadvantage on Dexterity saving throws. This effect lasts for 1 minute or until you fall unconscious. After using this feature, you cannot use it again for another 24 hours.

    Raki Raki No Mi (Luck)

    Devil Fruit, Rare

    Type. Environment Alterer Paramecia

    Fruit appearance. The Raki Raki No Mi is a radiant golden star fruit with glimmering star patterns etched onto its skin.

    Description. The Raki Raki No Mi grants its user the power to manipulate luck, bringing fortune to themselves or casting misfortune onto others, turning the user into a "Luck Human".

    Sea Weakness. You are weak to water and seastone.

    Luck Control. You learn the guidance cantrip. Additionally, as a bonus action on your turn, you can spend 3 devil fruit charges to use a "Luck" die. Roll a d20 and record the number rolled. For the next hour, you can replace any attack roll, saving throw, or ability check made by you or a creature that you can see with the result of this dice. You must choose to do so before the roll, and you can replace a roll in this way only once per turn. You can only hold one Luck die at a time.

    Luck Thief. As an action, you can spend 1 devil fruit charge to touch a creature within 5 feet of you. It must succeed on a Wisdom saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC. On a failed save, the creature has disadvantage on one roll of your choice per round while you have advantage one roll of your choice per round, for 1d4 rounds. The creature can make another Wisdom save at the end of each of its turn to end this effect on itself and you.

    Spells (Fortune Techniques). This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Bane (1 charge, and can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), Bless (1 charge, and can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), Fortune's Favor (2 charges), Bestow Curse (3 charges), Circle of Power (5 charges), or Deadly Misfortune (Contagion; 5 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

    Awakening (Wheel of Fortune). Once you've awakened your power, as an action, you can create a zone of intensified fortune within a 30-foot radius centered on yourself. While inside this zone, you and up to four other allied creatures roll a d20 at the start of their turn and must record the result. Until the start of its next turn, any creature that makes this roll can use the result in place any any attack roll, saving throw, or ability check made by itself or another creature it can see inside the zone. It must choose to do so before the roll, and it can replace a roll in this way only once per turn. This effect lasts for 1 minute or until you fall unconscious. After using this feature, you cannot use it again for another 24 hours.

    CHAPTER 2 | RARE PARAMECIA

    \page

    Peto Peto No Mi (Mind Control)

    Devil Fruit, Rare

    Type. Substance Generator Paramecia

    Fruit appearance. The Peto Peto no Mi is a deep green fruit, covered in a slimy gel-like substance that has an eerie shine to it. Its appearance is reminiscent of an overripe lime, with multiple wrinkles and soft spots, yet it glistens in any form of light.

    Description. The Peto Peto No Mi grants its user the ability to control the minds of living creatures by placing upon them a green, gel-like collar, turning the user into a "Mind Control Human".

    Sea Weakness. You are weak to water and seastone.

    Collar Creation. As an action, you can produce a green gel-like collar from your hand. Placing this collar on a creature requires a melee or ranged Devil Fruit spell attack if they resist. Alternatively, a willing creature can be given a collar without the need for a roll. Any creature wearing this collar has disadvantage on any Enchantment spells you cast on it. Escaping the collar requires a successful DC 20 Dexterity check. Breaking them requires a successful DC 20 Strength check. A collar has 15 hit points and 20 AC. If you fall unconscious, all collars are destroyed.

    Enthrall. Once a creature has a collar on them, you can use an action to attempt to control it. The creature must make a Wisdom saving throw against your Devil Fruit DC. On a failed save, the creature is under your control and charmed by you for up to 1 hour, during which they will follow any verbal commands. If the creature receives a command that might result in danger for itself, it gets another saving throw to resist the command. Removing the collar ends the control effect.

    Spells (Mental Techniques). This devil fruit power has 9 charges. Any spell cast using this feature must target creatures wearing one of your collars. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Command (1 charge, and can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), Suggestion (2 charges), Enthrall (2 charges), Fast Friends (3 charges), Confusion (4 charges), Dominate Beast (4 charges), Compulsion (4 charges), Dominate Person (5 charges), or Geas (5 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

    Awakening (Master Manipulator). Once you've awakened your power, you can control multiple creatures simultaneously. As an action, you can produce and place special collars which emerge out of the ground on up to 5 creatures within 30 feet of you. This feature requires each creature wearing one of your collars to immediately make a Wisdom saving throw against your Devil Fruit DC or be controlled as per the Enthrall feature. These awakened collars last for 1 minute or until you fall unconscious, after which they are destroyed. After using this feature, you cannot use it again for another 24 hours.

    Hemo Hemo No Mi (Blood Manipulation)

    Devil Fruit, Rare

    Type. Environment Alterer Paramecia

    Fruit appearance. The Hemo Hemo no Mi resembles a deep crimson pomegranate with darker vein-like patterns crisscrossing its surface.

    Description. The Hemo Hemo No Mi grants its user the chilling ability to manipulate and control blood, both their own and that of others. This fearsome power crowns the user as the "Blood Bender".

    Sea Weakness. You are weak to water and seastone.

    Hematokinesis. You learn the infestation cantrip, no material components required, which allows you to control the blood in other living creatures.

    Blood Drain. With a touch, you can drain the vitality of a creature. When you hit a creature with a melee weapon or melee spell attack, you can spend 1 devil fruit charge to absorb its blood. On a hit, the target takes an additional 2d6 necrotic damage, and you regain hit points equal to half the necrotic damage dealt.

    Vascular Control. If you can see a creature that's been injured (and thus is bleeding) within the past minute, you can attempt to control their movement by manipulating their blood flow. As an action, choose a creature within 60 feet. They must succeed on a Constitution saving throw against your Devil Fruit DC or be paralyzed until the end of your next turn. Alternatively, on a failed save you can instead have the creature use all of its movement to move in a direction of your choice during its turn.

    Spells (Blood Techniques). This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Inflict Wounds (Can be casted at higher levels by spending additional charges; 1 charge), Ray of Enfeeblement (2 charges), Hold Person (2 charges), Blood Bridge (as Life Transference; 3 charges), Vampiric Touch (3 charges), Staunch (as Stoneskin, but the user's skin becomes iron-hard due to concentrated blood; 4 charges), Blight (4 charges), Blood Puppet (as Dominate Person but only works on bleeding targets; 5 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

    Awakening (Total Blood Puppet). Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to cast Finger of Death, without expending a spell slot or material components, as you ravage the target's body with your blood control. You can't use this action again for another 24 hours.

    CHAPTER 2 | RARE PARAMECIA

    \page

    Ton Ton no Mi (Ton)

    Devil Fruit, Rare

    Type. Body Enhancer Paramecia

    Fruit appearance. An extremely heavy, dark gray-colored cylindrical melon with a sturdy stem and swirls across its surface.

    Description. This fruit grants the user the ability to manipulate their weight without changing their size. At will, the user can become as light as a feather or as heavy as a ton, granting them significant advantages in combat and mobility.

    Sea Weakness. You are weak to water and seastone.

    Weight Manipulation. As an action, you can adjust your weight to 1 gram or 10,000 tons for 1 minute, or return to your regular weight. Changing your weight does not change your physical size or shape, and you return to your normal weight if you are knocked unconscious.

    • When you weigh 1 gram: Your movement speed doubles, you can move over water or fragile surfaces without breaking them, you don't take fall damage, and you make dexterity checks and saving throws at advantage but make strength checks and saving throws at disadvantage. Your jump distance is also tripled.
    • When you weigh 10,000 tons: Your melee attacks deal an extra 4d8 bludgeoning damage, your speed and jump distance is halved, and you make strength checks and saving throws at advantage but make dexterity checks and saving throws at disadvantage. You are also immune to being pushed or pulled against your will.

    Hell Vice. When you're in the air (such as from a jump or fall), as a part of your action to become 10,000 tons, you can also deliver a crushing blow to enemies below you. All creatures within a 15-foot radius from where you land must make a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (their choice) against your Devil Fruit save DC or take 8d10 bludgeoning damage and be knocked prone. If they succeed, they take half damage and aren't knocked prone. You do not take fall damage so long as you don't fall more than 30 feet as a part of this ability.

    Spells (Ton Techniques). This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Earth Tremor (while 10,000 tons; Self; 1 charge, and can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), Misty Step (while 1 gram; 2 charges), Erupting Earth (while 10,000 tons; Self; Doesn't affect you; 3 charges), Levitate (while 1 gram; Self; 3 charges), Destructive Wave (while 10,000 tons; 5 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

    Awakening (Final Vice). Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to cast Gravity Fissure at the 9th level, without expending a spell slot or material components. You can't use this action again for another 24 hours.

    Bigu Bigu No Mi (Growing in Size)

    Devil Fruit, Rare

    Type. Body Enhancer Paramecia

    Fruit appearance. The Bigu Bigu no Mi is a bulky fruit with an exterior resembling inflated, tight green skin, with sporadic, oversized pores.

    Description. The Bigu Bigu No Mi bestows upon its user the wondrous power to increase their size, transforming them into a colossal version of themselves and earning them the epithet of the "Giant Human".

    Sea Weakness. You are weak to water and seastone.

    Growing Might. As an action, you can increase your size up to gargantuan, along with anything you are wearing or carrying. This growth lasts for 10 minutes or until you end it as a bonus action. While grown, you increase the weapon damage dice on Strength-based weapons you wield by 1d4 for each size category greater you are than medium, and you gain advantage on Strength checks and Strength saving throws.

    Extended Reach. Your reach increases by 5 feet for each size category greater than medium you are when you are enlarged using your Growing Might, enabling you to grasp and interact with objects or targets from a distance.

    Spells (Growth Techniques). This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Earth Tremor (while at increased size; 1 charge, and can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), Erupting Earth (while at increased size; Self; Doesn't affect you; 3 charges), Destructive Wave (while at increased size; 5 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

    Awakening (Titanic Surge). Upon awakening, as an action, you can increase the sizes of up to four allies using your Growing Might feature, as well as giving them the benefits of your Extended Reach feature. Additionally, you can increase the size of any nonmagical object that isn't being held or worn within 60 feet of you to garganutan. This effect lasts for 1 minute, or until you fall unconscious. After using this feature, you cannot use it again for another 24 hours.

    CHAPTER 2 | RARE PARAMECIA

    Mosa Mosa No Mi (Plant Growth)

    Devil Fruit, Rare

    Type. Environment Alterer Paramecia

    Fruit appearance. The Mosa Mosa no Mi resembles a small, lime-green melon with twisting vine patterns wrapping around its surface.

    Description. The Mosa Mosa No Mi grants its user the incredible ability to stimulate and control rapid plant growth, from the tiniest of seeds to the mightiest of trees. The user becomes known as the "Plant Human."

    Sea Weakness. You are weak to water and seastone.

    Plants Growth. You learn the Thorn Whip cantrip. Additionallly as a bonus action, you can cause any seeds or plants within a 10-foot radius to grow at an accelerated rate. The plants can be manipulated to grow in shapes or directions you desire. You can use this to make the area difficult terrain, produce 100 feet of rope-like vines, or double the size of a plant (up to gargantuan).

    Nature's Embrace. You can spend an action to summon thick vines and foliage from the ground or nearby vegetation to restrain enemies. Creatures within 10 feet of you must make a Strength saving throw against your Devil Fruit DC or be restrained. They can repeat the saving throw at the end of each of their turns to break free.

    Spells (Growth Techniques). This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Entangle (1 charge), Goodberry (1 charge), Locate Animals or Plants (plants only; 2 charges), Spike Growth (2 charges), Plant Growth (3 charges), Speak with Plants (3 charges), Grasping Vine (4 charges), Awaken (plants only; 5 charges), or Wrath of Nature (5 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

    Awakening (Living Forest). Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to cast Druid Grove (casting time 1 action), without expending a spell slot or material components, as you awaken the plant life around you. You can't use this action again for another 24 hours.

    Shiku Shiku No Mi (Sickness)

    Devil Fruit, Rare

    Type. Substance Generator Paramecia

    Fruit appearance. The Shiku Shiku no Mi is a sickly green, bulbous fruit with purple pulsating veins.

    Description. The Shiku Shiku No Mi allows its user to induce and control various diseases, making the user a "Disease Human." The wielder can cause mild to severe illnesses in targets, but also has the unique ability to draw upon the strength of the diseases they control.

    Sea Weakness. You are weak to water and seastone.

    Disease Immunity. You are immune to all diseases, both mundane and magical.

    Infectious Touch. As an action, you can touch a creature, forcing them to make a Constitution saving throw against you Devil Fruit save DC. On a failed save, the target contracts a disease of your choice (it must save against your Devil Fruit DC for each disease):

    • Cackle Fever. See "sample diseases" in standard 5e DMG.
    • Sewer Plague. See "sample diseases" in standard 5e DMG.
    • Sight Rot. See "sample diseases" in standard 5e DMG.
    • Hormone Reversal. A creature's sex is swapped after 1d4 hours. A creature can attempt to recover from this condition by repeating the Constitution save after it finishes a long rest. Once it recovers from this disease, it becomes immune to it.

    Pandemic Wave. As an action, you can spend 3 devil fruit charges to unleash a wave of disease in a 30-foot radius. Every creature within the radius must make a Constitution saving throw or contract a disease of your choice (see Infectious Touch).

    Spells (Pathogenic Techniques). This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Ray of Sickness (1 charge, and can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), Sudden Fever (Phantasmal Force; 2 charges), Extreme Fever (Phantasmal Killer; 4 charges), Blight (4 charges), Contagion (5 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

    Awakening (Pestilence Wave). Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to cast Contagion, without expending a spell slot or material components, on each creature of your choice within 30 feet of you. You can't use this action again for another 24 hours.

    CHAPTER 2 | RARE PARAMECIA

    \page

    Inu Inu no Mi, Model: Wolf

    Devil Fruit, Rare

    Type. Standard Zoan

    Fruit appearance. This devil fruit appears as a gray and black peach with thick fuzz across its surface.

    Description. This zoan devil fruit allows its user to transform into a large wolf.

    Sea Weakness. You are weak to water and seastone.

    Beast Shape. As an action, you are able to transform into a Dire Wolf from the standard 5th Edition Monster Manual. You follow the rules given in Chapter 7 under "Designing a Zoan Devil Fruit Sheet" in the One Piece Dungeons and Devil Fruits PHB.

    Hybrid Form. You can use your action to enter a "hybrid" zoan state, combining a mix of qualities from both your humanoid form and beast form together for a temporary period of time. You follow the rules given in Chapter 7 under "Designing a Zoan Devil Fruit Sheet" in the One Piece Dungeons and Devil Fruits PHB.

    Awakening. Upon the awakening of your Zoan Devil Fruit power, when you enter your Hybrid Form, you can temporarily enter your Awakened State, which lasts for 1 minute.

    While your Awakened State is active, your hit point maximum and hit points increase by 50, your weapon attacks and unarmed strike attacks deal extra damage of their primary damage type equal to your character level, and you are able to select an additional hybrid form option. Furthermore, at the start of each of your turns for the duration of this state, you regain hit points equivalent to your character level + your Constitution modifier.

    Should the duration of your Awakened State expire, you hold the option to extend its span for an additional minute, at the cost of incurring a level of exhaustion. If needed, you can further extend this state by enduring an extra level of exhaustion for each additional minute. These levels of exhaustion can only be removed by completing a long rest.

    Once your Awakened State ends, it can't be activated again for another 24 hours.

    Should the duration of your Awakened State expire, you hold the option to extend its span for an additional minute, at the cost of incurring a level of exhaustion. If needed, you can further extend this state by enduring an extra level of exhaustion for each additional minute. These levels of exhaustion can only be removed by completing a long rest.

    Once your Awakened State ends, it can't be activated again for another 24 hours.

    Leopard

    Large beast, unaligned

    • Armor Class 12
    • Hit Points 37(5d10 + 10)
    • Speed 60 ft.
    STR DEX CON INT WIS CHA
    17 (+3) 15 (+2) 14 (+2) 3 (-4) 12 (+1) 8 (-1)
    ___
    - Skills Perception +3, Stealth +6
    - Senses darkvision 60 ft., passive Perception 13
    - Challenge 1 (200 XP)
    ___
    Keen Smell. The leopard has advantage on Wisdom (Perception) checks that rely on smell.

    Pounce. If the leopard moves at least 20 ft. straight toward a creature and then hits it with a claw attack on the same turn, that target must succeed on a DC 13 Strength saving throw or be knocked prone. If the target is prone, the leopard can make one bite attack against it as a bonus action.

    Actions

    Bite. Melee Weapon Attack: +5 to hit, reach 5ft., one target. Hit 8 (1d10 + 3) piercing damage

    Claw. Melee Weapon Attack: +5 to hit, reach 5ft., one target. Hit 7 (1d8 + 3) slashing damage

    CHAPTER 2 | RARE ZOAN

    \page

    Guwa Guwa no Mi, Model: Toad

    Devil Fruit, Rare

    Type. Standard Zoan

    Fruit appearance. This devil fruit appears as a vine of green grapes with light-colored swirls across their surface.

    Description. This zoan devil fruit allows its user to transform into a giant toad.

    Sea Weakness. You are weak to water and seastone.

    Beast Shape. As an action, you are able to transform into a Giant Toad from the standard 5th Edition Monster Manual. You follow the rules given in Chapter 7 under "Designing a Zoan Devil Fruit Sheet" in the One Piece Dungeons and Devil Fruits PHB.

    Hybrid Form. You can use your action to enter a "hybrid" zoan state, combining a mix of qualities from both your humanoid form and beast form together for a temporary period of time. You follow the rules given in Chapter 7 under "Designing a Zoan Devil Fruit Sheet" in the One Piece Dungeons and Devil Fruits PHB.

    Awakening. Upon the awakening of your Zoan Devil Fruit power, when you enter your Hybrid Form, you can temporarily enter your Awakened State, which lasts for 1 minute.

    While your Awakened State is active, your hit point maximum and hit points increase by 50, your weapon attacks and unarmed strike attacks deal extra damage of their primary damage type equal to your character level, and you are able to select an additional hybrid form option. Furthermore, at the start of each of your turns for the duration of this state, you regain hit points equivalent to your character level + your Constitution modifier.

    Should the duration of your Awakened State expire, you hold the option to extend its span for an additional minute, at the cost of incurring a level of exhaustion. If needed, you can further extend this state by enduring an extra level of exhaustion for each additional minute. These levels of exhaustion can only be removed by completing a long rest.

    Once your Awakened State ends, it can't be activated again for another 24 hours.

    Beast Shape. As an action, you are able to transform into an Giant Eagle from the standard 5th Edition Monster Manual. You follow the rules given in Chapter 7 under "Designing a Zoan Devil Fruit Sheet" in the One Piece Dungeons and Devil Fruits PHB.

    Hybrid Form. You can use your action to enter a "hybrid" zoan state, combining a mix of qualities from both your humanoid form and beast form together for a temporary period of time. You follow the rules given in Chapter 7 under "Designing a Zoan Devil Fruit Sheet" in the One Piece Dungeons and Devil Fruits PHB.

    Awakening. Upon the awakening of your Zoan Devil Fruit power, when you enter your Hybrid Form, you can temporarily enter your Awakened State, which lasts for 1 minute.

    While your Awakened State is active, your hit point maximum and hit points increase by 50, your weapon attacks and unarmed strike attacks deal extra damage of their primary damage type equal to your character level, and you are able to select an additional hybrid form option. Furthermore, at the start of each of your turns for the duration of this state, you regain hit points equivalent to your character level + your Constitution modifier.

    Should the duration of your Awakened State expire, you hold the option to extend its span for an additional minute, at the cost of incurring a level of exhaustion. If needed, you can further extend this state by enduring an extra level of exhaustion for each additional minute. These levels of exhaustion can only be removed by completing a long rest.

    Once your Awakened State ends, it can't be activated again for another 24 hours.

    Trampling Charge. If the hippopotamus moves at least 20 feet straight toward a creature and then hits it with a slam attack on the same turn, that target must succeed on a DC 14 Strength saving throw or be knocked prone.     Amphibious. The turtle can breathe air and water.

    Stable. Whenever an effect knocks the turtle prone, it can make a DC 10 Constitution saving throw to avoid being knocked prone. A prone turtle is upside down. To stand up, it must succeed on a DC 10 Dexterity check on its turn and then use all its movement for that turn.

    Actions

    Bite. Melee Weapon Attack: +6 to hit, reach 5ft., one target. Hit (3d6 + 4) slashing damage.

    CHAPTER 2 | RARE ZOAN

    \page

    Ushi Ushi no Mi, Model: Bison

    Devil Fruit, Rare

    Type. Standard Zoan

    Fruit appearance. This devil fruit appears as a large poofy yellow melon with dark swirls across its surface.

    Description. This zoan devil fruit allows its user to transform into a bison.

    Sea Weakness. You are weak to water and seastone.

    Beast Shape. As an action, you are able to transform into an Aurochs (reflavored as a bison) from Volo's Guide to Monsters. You follow the rules given in Chapter 7 under "Designing a Zoan Devil Fruit Sheet" in the One Piece Dungeons and Devil Fruits PHB.

    Hybrid Form. You can use your action to enter a "hybrid" zoan state, combining a mix of qualities from both your humanoid form and beast form together for a temporary period of time. You follow the rules given in Chapter 7 under "Designing a Zoan Devil Fruit Sheet" in the One Piece Dungeons and Devil Fruits PHB.

    Awakening. Upon the awakening of your Zoan Devil Fruit power, when you enter your Hybrid Form, you can temporarily enter your Awakened State, which lasts for 1 minute.

    While your Awakened State is active, your hit point maximum and hit points increase by 50, your weapon attacks and unarmed strike attacks deal extra damage of their primary damage type equal to your character level, and you are able to select an additional hybrid form option. Furthermore, at the start of each of your turns for the duration of this state, you regain hit points equivalent to your character level + your Constitution modifier.

    Should the duration of your Awakened State expire, you hold the option to extend its span for an additional minute, at the cost of incurring a level of exhaustion. If needed, you can further extend this state by enduring an extra level of exhaustion for each additional minute. These levels of exhaustion can only be removed by completing a long rest.

    Once your Awakened State ends, it can't be activated again for another 24 hours.

    CHAPTER 2 | RARE ZOAN

    \page

    Very Rare Devil Fruits

    Nikyu Nikyu no Mi (Paw Repel)

    Devil Fruit, Very Rare

    Type. Body Enhancer Paramecia

    Fruit appearance. A light-beige, paw-shaped fruit with swirls and dark spots across its surface.

    Description. Grants the user the ability to repel anything they touch with their paw-padded palms, including intangible concepts such as pain and fatigue, by using the paw pads on their palms.

    Sea Weakness. You are weak to water and seastone.

    Paw Push. If you take the Attack action to shove a target and push it back, you can choose to push it back 30 feet using your paw-padded palms. If a pushed target strikes a solid surface, the target takes 3 (1d6) bludgeoning damage for every 10 feet it was pushed. If the target is thrown at another creature, that creature must succeed on a Dexterity saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC or take the same damage and be knocked prone.

    Additionally, you may expend additional devil fruit charges to increase the distance the creature is pushed as a part of this attack. If you do so, you push the creature back an additional 10 feet per devil fruit charge expended, up to 100 feet in total.

    Paw Cannon. You have the ability to repel the air around you, allowing you to fire paw-shaped air shockwaves. As an action, you can make a ranged spell attack against a target within 120 feet. On a hit, the creature takes 4d6 thunder damage and must succeed on a Strength saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC or be knocked prone. You can spend 1 or more devil fruit charges to increase the damage of this attack, dealing an extra 1d6 damage per charge expended, up to 12d6 total thunder damage.

    Defensive Repel. When targeted and hit by an attack, you can use your reaction and spend 7 devil fruit charges to attempt to repel the attack, causing the damage to become 0. The attacker must make a Dexterity saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC. On a failed save, the attacker takes half of the damage they would have dealt to you, as the attack is redirected back to them.

    Ursus Shock. As an action, you may spend 1 or more devil fruit charges to concentrate a large volume of air into your palms, allowing you to unleash it out as a devastating shockwave centered on a point within 120 feet that you can see. If you do so, you target each creature in a 10-foot-radius sphere centered on that point must succeed on a Constitution saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC. A creature takes 3d10 thunder damage on a failed save, or half as much damage on a successful one. A creature made of inorganic material such as stone, crystal, or metal has disadvantage on this saving throw. A nonmagical object that isn’t being worn or carried also takes the damage if it’s in the shockwave’s area. The shockwave's damage increases by 1d10 and it's radius increases by 5 feet for each additional devil fruit charge expended over 1, dealing up to 11d10 thunder damage and having up to a 50-foot radius in total.

    Pain Repel. As an action, you may expend 1 or more devil fruit charges to touch a creature and repel the pain from its body. If you do so, the target creature regains 1d10 hit points for every devil fruit charge spent. This ability has no effect on undead or constructs. Additionally, the repelled pain congeals and forms into a 10-foot-radius bubble in an empty space next to the target, and stores a number of pain equal to the amount healed from the target. The bubble lasts for up to 1 hour or until it pops. As an action, you may push the bubble up to 30 feet away from you by touching it. If you push the bubble into a creature, that creature must make a Dexterity saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC, and the bubble pops. The creature takes the amount of stored pain in necrotic damage on a failed save, or half as much damage on a successful one.

    Extended Travel Repel. As an action, you can touch a creature and spend 7 devil fruit charges to attempt to teleport it to a location by repelling it at extreme speeds. The creature must make a Constitution saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC. A willing creature automatically fails this save. On a failure, the creature is teleported to a place you are aware of, landing in a random empty space in the region of the DM's choice. If no target destination is given, the target is teleported to a random location of the DM's choosing in the direction it is pushed, at least 1 mile away. On a successful save, the creature is instead repelled 30 feet away from you, as per your Paw Push ability.

    Spells (Repelling Techniques). This devil fruit power has 13 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Misty Step (2 charges), Air Bubble (2 charges), Thunder Step (3 charges), Wind Wall (3 charges), Gravity Sinkhole (4 charges), Destructive Wave (5 charges), Far step (5 charges), Scatter (6 charges), or Teleport (7 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

    Awakening (Extended Group Vacation). Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to target up to 5 creatures within 30 feet of you, threatening to repel them at extreme speeds away from you. A target creature must make a Constitution saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC. On a failure, the creature is subjected to your Extended Travel Repel feature. On a success, the creature is instead repelled up to 30 feet away from you, as per your Paw Push ability.

    After using this feature, you cannot use it again for another 24 hours.

    CHAPTER 3 | VERY RARE PARAMECIA

    \page

    Kira Kira no Mi (Diamond)

    Devil Fruit, Very Rare

    Type. Body Enhancer Paramecia

    Fruit appearance. A shimmering blue berry with multifaceted crystalline surfaces.

    Description. This devil fruit empowers its user with the ability to transform or harden any part of their body into diamond.

    Sea Weakness. You are weak to water and seastone.

    Sharpened Diamond Body. As a bonus action, you can transform any part of your body into a melee weapon of your choice. This can range from turning an arm into a diamond longsword, fingers into dagger-like diamond blades, or even combining your arms or legs into a diamond greatclub. Weapons you create have the same properties as their normal counterparts but are considered magical for the purpose of overcoming resistance. You can use this part of your body as a weapon attack, and you are proficient with it. You can only use one weapon active this way at a time, and can dismiss it using a bonus action.

    Diamond Skin. Your AC can’t be less than 20, regardless of what kind of armor you are wearing. By spending 1 devil fruit charge as a bonus action, you can gain a +2 bonus to your AC for up to 1 minute or until you fall unconscious (this effect doesn't stack).

    Brilliant Punk. You can spend a bonus action to bolster the next melee weapon attack you make during your turn with your diamond body. On a hit, the attack deals an extra 2d6 damage of the weapon's damage type. Additionally, if the target is a creature, it must succeed on a Strength saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC or be pushed 10 feet away from you and knocked prone.

    Spells (Diamond Techniques). This devil fruit power has 13 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Thunder Step (3 charges, and can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), Stoneskin (Self; 4 charges), Destructive Wave (5 charges), or Tenser's Transformation (6 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

    Awakening (Brilliant Wave). Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to unleash a mighty earth shockwave affecting any creature standing on the ground within 60 feet of you. Any creature hit by the shockwave must make a Constitution saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC. On a failed save, a creature takes 10d10 bludgeoning damage and 10d10 thunder damage, and is knocked prone. A creature that succeeds on its saving throw takes half as much damage and isn’t knocked prone. Additionally, immediately after you use this ability, the ground within 60 feet of you becomes extremely hard and diamond-like for 1 minute, and cannot be destroyed or affected by any spells or other effects for the duation. Once used, you can't use this action again for another 24 hours.

    CHAPTER 3 | VERY RARE PARAMECIA

    \page

    Goru Goru no Mi (Gold Manipulation)

    Devil Fruit, Very Rare

    Type. Environment Alterer Paramecia

    Fruit appearance. An extremely shiny golden pear, with cloud-like spiral patterns across its surface.

    Description. This devil fruit empowers its user with the ability to manipulate and move around massive amounts of gold telekinetically.

    Sea Weakness. You are weak to water and seastone.

    Chrysokinesis. You can use the Telekinesis and Levitate spells at will, without expending a spell slot, charge, or material components. You can only target objects made of gold and creatures wearing or holding gold items using these spells this way.

    Gold Manipulation. As an action, you can target any gold within 60 feet of you to form up to thirteen 5-foot diameter spheres worth of affected gold, allowing you to telekinetically control the gold (as if using the Telekinesis spell). You cannot have more than thirteen of these gold spheres under you control at once. You require 100,000 gold pieces or 400 gold bars (or ฿1,000,000,000 worth of gold) to form each individual 5-foot diameter sphere this way. Once you use this action, you cannot use it again for another 24 hours.

    Any gold being telekinetically controlled by this ability is considered liquid (but doesn't count against a Devil Fruit user's Sea Weakness) unless otherwise stated, and counts as difficult terrain when moved through in its liquid state. Creatures will suffocate inside liquid gold if they remain inside it. Any gold forcibly moved 60 feet away from you while being telekinetically controlled returns to an empty space you can see within 60 feet of you at the start of your next turn. Additionally, while the spheres are under your telekinetic control, you can spend an action to use one of the following effects on the gold during your turn:

    • Combine/Separate: You can combine the volumes of the gold spheres to form a larger mass of liquefied gold with a total volume no greater than the total volumes of your currently controlled gold, or split the mass back apart into independent 5-foot diameter spheres.

    • Slam: You can slam a single 5-foot diameter sphere of gold into a creature you can see within 30 feet of you. The target must succeed on a Dexterity saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC, or take 3d10 bludgeoning damage.

    • Armory: You can use a single 5-foot diameter sphere of gold to form any weapon or armor of your choice. You are proficient with any gold weapon or armor you use, and ignore strength requirements to use it. Weapons you create have the same properties as their normal counterparts but are considered magical for the purpose of overcoming resistance. The gold cannot be controlled or used while it is used as a weapon or piece of armor, unless you reform it back into a sphere a bonus action.

    • Bind: You can use a single 5-foot diameter sphere of gold to target a creature within 30 feet of you. The creature must succeed on a Strength saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC, or become restrained by the gold for 1 minute or until it breaks free (escape DC equal to your Devil Fruit save DC). The gold cannot be controlled or used while it restrains a creature, unless you free the creature from it as a bonus action.

    • Animate: You use one sphere of gold to construct a solid Gold Golem (as Iron Golem; stats found in the standard 5th Edition Monster Manual). It is under your control, and it understands and obeys your spoken commands. When it falls to 0 hit points or otherwise gets destroyed, so does the gold sphere used to construct it. You can only have one Gold Golem activate at a time, and once you create one you can't create anohter one for 24 hours.

    • Collect: You condense the gold into tiny rings you collect, one ring per 5-foot diameter sphere of gold. You gain 1 devil fruit charge per ring collected, not exceeding 13 total charges, but can no longer affect the collected gold telepathically using your Gold Manipulation feature until you re-activate the feature.

    Spells (Golden Techniques). This devil fruit power has 13 maximum charges, but you start with none. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Golden Burst (as Thunderous Smite; 1 charge), Golden Arms (as Arms of Hadar; 1 charge, and can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), Gold Wave (as Tidal Wave, made of liquid gold; 3 charges), Golden Tentacles (as Evard's Black Tentacles; 4 charges), Golden Hand (as Bigby's Hand; 5 charges), Golden Wall (as Wall of Stone; 5 charges), Flesh to Gold (as Flesh to Stone; 6 charges), and Golden Inferno (as Firestorm; 7 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges when you use your "Collect" ability. All material created using these spells return back to the original gold value used to create the devil fruit charges to fuel it after the spell's duration ends.

    Awakening (Gold Splash). Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to temporarily alchemically manifest gold from the environment, which you can control telepathically. When you do so, you can use this gold to cast Tsunami, with a 1 action casting time. After the Tsunami ends, the gold returns back to mundane, nonmagical materials. Once used, you can't use this action again for another 24 hours.

    CHAPTER 3 | VERY RARE PARAMECIA

    \page

    Mochi Mochi no Mi (Mochi)

    Devil Fruit, Very Rare

    Type. Special Paramecia

    Fruit appearance. A creamy white fruit with a swirl pattern across its surface. It appears to have a pinched off, flattened foot toward the bottom of it.

    Description. This devil fruit allows the user to create, control, and transform into mochi

    Sea Weakness. You are weak to water and seastone.

    Mochi Body. You are immune to bludgeoning, piercing, and slashing from nonmagical attacks, as physical objects pass through your mochi body. Additionally, you can move across Difficult Terrain created by mochi or sticky surfaces without spending extra Movement.

    Mochi Creation. As a mochi being, you are able to produce and control mochi in various ways. Any mochi produced with this devil fruit is thick and viscous enough to not be considered water to devil fruit users, but creatures fully submerged in mochi will suffocate and drown normally as if they are underwater. You are immune to suffocating in your own mochi.

    You can spend 1 devil fruit charge to cast create or destroy water as a 1st-level spell slot, without expending a spell slot or material components. Instead of producing or destroying water with this spell, you produce or destroy edible mochi that is much thicker than water in the same amount and volume. This mochi counts as food when consumed, but spoils after 24 hours. You may spend additional devil fruit charges to increase the level of this spell by 1 for every charge expended as a part of casting the spell. Additionally, you learn and can use the Shape Water cantrip on this mochi.

    Additionally, you can spend a bonus action to harden the mochi into a solid block of mochi which can expand up to a 10-by-10 ft cube, but counts as the same amount of food. A creature in the mochi's space when it expands is pushed out safely to the nearest space.

    Mochi Reach. You learn the mage hand cantrip. Additionally, when you make a melee weapon attack on your turn, you can make its reach extend up to 30 feet by stretching your mochi limbs.

    Mochi Weapon. As a bonus action, you can transform any part of your body into a melee weapon of your choice. This can range from turning an arm into a longsword, fingers into dagger-like blades, or even combining your arms or legs into a greatclub. Weapons you create have the same properties as their normal counterparts but are considered magical for the purpose of overcoming resistance. You can use this part of your body as a weapon attack, and you are proficient with it. You can only use one weapon active this way at a time, and can dismiss it using a bonus action. When you hit a creature with a melee weapon created this way while it is within 5 feet of you, it must make a Strength saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC or become grappled by you as it sticks to the mochi surface.

    Spells (Mochi Techniques). This devil fruit power has 13 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Buzz Cut Mochi (as Zephyr Strike; 1 charge), Willow Mochi (as Arms of Hadar; 1 charge, and can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), Burning Mochi (as Scorching Ray; 2 charges, and can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), Mochi Grasp (as Maximillian's Earthen Grasp; 2 charges), Wall of Mochi (as Wall of Water, but made of mochi; 3 charges), Mochi Tentacles (as Evard's Black Tentacles; 4 charges), Mochi Hand (Bigby's Hand; 5 charges), or Mochi Shield (as Fizban's Platinum Shield; Self; 6 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

    Awakening (Unstoppable Donuts). Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to temporarily manifest large amounts of concentrated mochi from the environment, which you can control telepathically to create two floating fists which emerge from mochi donuts. When you do so, the two large hands appear within 120 feet of you at a point you can see, which act as Bigby's Hand (no concentration required), and last for 1 minute or until you fall unconscious. You can use an action on your turn to create an additional hand this way, which appears within 120 feet of you, and lasts until the duration of this ability ends. As a bonus action, you can move and act with any number of mochi hands you control at once, as per the spell description of Bigby's Hand for each. Once used, you can't use this awakening again for another 24 hours.

    CHAPTER 3 | VERY RARE PARAMECIA

    \page

    Bari Bari no Mi (Barrier)

    Devil Fruit, Very Rare

    Type. Substance Generator Paramecia

    Fruit appearance. An emerald green melon with a swirl pattern across its surface and a crescent-shaped stem. Its surface is extremely hard, and very difficult to bite through.

    Description. This devil fruit allows the user to create and manipulate magical barriers made of force.

    Sea Weakness. You are weak to water and seastone.

    Barrier Creation. As an action, you can cast Wall of Force at will without expending a spell slot, charges, or material components. However, when you cast it using this feature, you can only produce one 10-by-10 foot panel or a 5-foot diameter sphere centered on you with it.

    Barrier Crash. While concentrating on a Wall of Force barrier you have created using this devil fruit power, you can spend an action to push it up to 30 feet in any direction, or until it collides with an unmovable object or terrain. Anything in the path of the moving barrier must make a Strength saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC, as the barrier slams against it. On a failure, the target is knocked prone, takes 2d8 force damage, and is pushed by the barrier up to the total distance you move it. On a success, it is only pushed by the barrier. If a creature is squished between your barrier and another object and fails the saving throw, it instead takes 4d8 force damage and is restrained until it breaks free (escape DC equal to your Devil Fruit save DC). On a success or if the creature breaks free, it is pushed out to the nearest empty space that your barrier isn't pushing against.

    Barrierbility. As an action, you can manipulate any active Wall of Force you have created to rearrange its panels into a shape of your choice, so long as each panel is still connected to another panel. For example, you can reform it into a staircase with each step being an individual panel of the wall. Any creature or object in the path of the shifting wall is not pushed or damaged by it.

    Barrier Fist. Once per turn when you hit a creature with a melee weapon attack, you can expend 1 devil fruit charge to deal an 2d8 force damage to the target, and it must succeed on a Strength saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC or you can knock it prone. You can expend additional devil fruit charges to deal another 1d8 force damage per additional charge expended, up to a total of 10d8 force damage.

    Spells (Barrier Techniques). This devil fruit power has 13 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Otiluke's Resilient Sphere (4 charges), Wall of Force (5 charges), Barrier Hand (as Bigby's Hand; 5 charges), or Forcecage (7 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

    Awakening (Gigabarrier). Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to temporarily manifest large amounts of energy from the environment, which you can then form and reshape into a massive barrier. When you do so, you cast a special Wall of Force, without expending a spell slot or material components. This special wall of force can have up to a hundred panels, and its radius is up to 100 feet instead. Once used, you can't use this awakening again for another 24 hours.

    CHAPTER 3 | VERY RARE PARAMECIA

    \page

    Jiki Jiki no Mi (Magnetism)

    Devil Fruit, Very Rare

    Type. Environment Alterer Paramecia

    Fruit appearance. A stainless steel fruit with tons of bolt-shaped barbs and cloud-like swirls across its surface. It has a yellow coil wrapping around it up to the stem, which appears like a bolt of lightning.

    Description. This devil fruit allows the user to control the magnetism and control metallic objects using magnetic forces.

    Sea Weakness. You are weak to water and seastone.

    Magnetokinesis. You can use the Telekinesis and Levitate spells at will, without expending a spell slot, charge, or material components. You can only target objects made of metal and creatures wearing or holding metal or metallic items using these spells this way.

    Magnetic Repel. When targeted and hit by an attack from a weapon or ammo which is made of metal, you can use your reaction and spend 7 devil fruit charges to attempt to repel the attack, causing the damage to become 0. The attacker must make a Dexterity saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC. On a failed save, the attacker takes half of the damage they would have dealt to you, as the attack is redirected back to them.

    Magnetic Assembly. As an action, you can attract a large amount of metal within 120 feet of you toward your body to assemble onto your body. You must spend 1 devil fruit charge for every 5-foot square of metal you attract and assemble onto your body. For each square of metal you assemble onto you, you gain 10 temporary hit points (which only stacks with each additional shadow absorbed) up to a maximum of 30, your weapon attacks deal an extra 1d4 damage (up to a maximum bonus of 3d4), your reach with melee weapons extends by 5 feet (up to a 15 foot total bonus), and your size increases by one (up to gargantuan). While this form is active, you have advantage on strength checks and saving throws. When you lose all temporary hit points granted by this ability, the metal you assembled is destroyed, and this ability ends.

    Electromagnetic Cannon. As an action, you can spend 3 devil fruit charges to create a large electromagnetic cannon from metal around you. When you do so, you can fire a beam of electromagnetic energy forming a line of 100 feet long and 5 feet wide out from you in a direction you choose. Each creature in the line must make a Strength saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC. A creature takes 6d6 bludgeoning damage on a failed save and is pushed back 20 feet away from you, or half as much damage on a successful one and isn't pushed. You can spend additional devil fruit charges to increase the bludgeoning damage by 1d6 and the push distance by 10 feet for each additional charge spent, up to a total of 12d6 bludgeoning damage and 80 feet.

    Spells (Magnetic Techniques). This devil fruit power has 13 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Catapult (targeting metal; 1 charges, and can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), Cloud of Daggers (2 charges, and can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), Fly (Self; 3 charges), Conjure Barrage (3 charges), Conjure Volley (5 charges), Scrap Metal Hand (as Bigby's Hand; 5 charges), Blade Barrier (6 charges), or Reverse Gravity (only affecting metallic objects and creatures wearing metal; 7 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

    Awakening (Magnetic Assignment). Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to mark two targets, which can be objects or creatures you can see within 120 feet of you, which causes them to become magnetically attracted to each other, even if they aren't made of metal or wearing metal. This magnetic attraction lasts for 1 minute, or until you fall unconscious. While these two targets are magnetically attracted to each other this way, each target at the start of each of its turns must make a Strength saving throw against your Devil Fruit save. On a failure, it is magnetically pulled up to 120 feet toward the other target, taking 1d6 bludgeoning damage per 10 feet traveled, unless the target is already within 5 feet of it. A target that is slammed into by an object or creature this way must make a Dexterity saving throw, taking the same damage on a failure or half as much on a success. Alternatively, you may force a target that fails its strength saving throw on its turn to be pushed away from the other target, up to a 120 foot gap between the two targets. If it is pushed away this way and crashes into an object, it takes 1d6 bludgeoning damage per 10 feet traveled from the crash.

    Additionally, you may spend an action on subsequent turns for the duration to cause metalic objects in the area to crash into a target you have marked this way, forcing the target to make a Dexterity saving throw. On a failure, the target takes 8d6 bludgeoning damage and is knocked prone. On a success, the target takes half as much damage and isn't knocked prone. If both marked targets are within 5 feet of each other, both must make this saving throw.

    Once used, you can't use this awakening again for another 24 hours.

    CHAPTER 3 | VERY RARE PARAMECIA

    \page

    Doku Doku no Mi (Poison)

    Devil Fruit, Very Rare

    Type. Substance Generator Paramecia

    Fruit appearance. A reddish-purple pineapple with black skull and crossbones.

    Description. Allows the user to produce deadly poisons and toxins from their body that can be controlled.

    Sea Weakness. You are weak to water and seastone.

    Poison Resistance. You are immune to poison damage and the poisoned condition.

    Toxic Spray. You learn the Poison Spray and Acid Splash Cantrips. Any time you deal poison damage to a creature using this devil fruit's spells and cantrips, if the effect doesn't already inflict the poisoned condition, the creature is poisoned until the start of your next turn.

    Poisonous Vapor Aura. Any creature of your choice that starts its turn within 10 feet of you must succeed on a Constitution saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC or be poisoned until the start of the creature's next turn. You can activate or deactivate this aura as a bonus action.

    Poison Hydra Heads. As an action, you can expend 3 devil fruit charges to create three giant poisonous hydra heads which connect to your body. These heads last for 1 minute and require concentration (as if concentrating on a spell) to maintain. You can use a bonus action to send one of the hydra heads crashing toward one creature or object you can see within 60 feet of you. When you do so, make a ranged spell attack. On a hit, the target takes 4d12 poison damage. Whether you hit or miss, the head is expended. This ability ends early if all heads are expended.

    Alternatively, you can expend a head of this hydra as a bonus action to fly up to 60 feet toward an empty space you can see without spending any movement, traveling along the hydras neck to the target destination. If you land in a space midair, you fall.

    Spells (Poison Gas and Blast). This devil fruit power has 13 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Poison Armor (as armor of agathys, but dealing poison damage instead; 1 charge, and can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), Dragon's Breath (self; poison damage; 2 charges), Vitrolic Sphere (4 charges), Cloudkill (5 charges), Contagion (5 charges), Prismatic Spray (choosing between green or orange rays only; 7 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

    Awakening (Toxic Demon). Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to cast Poison Giant: Hell's Judgement^ (view Chapter 8 in the Dungeons and Devil Fruits PHB), without expending any charges or material components. You can’t use this action again for another 24 hours.

    CHAPTER 3 | VERY RARE PARAMECIA

    \page

    Zou Zou no Mi, Model: Mammoth

    Devil Fruit, Very Rare

    Type. Ancient Zoan

    Fruit appearance. This devil fruit appears as a massive brown apple with black furry stripes, and two white tusk-like stems.

    Description. This zoan devil fruit allows its user to transform into a mammoth.

    Sea Weakness. You are weak to water and seastone.

    Beast Shape. As an action, you are able to transform into a Mammoth from the standard 5th Edition Monster Manual. You follow the rules given in Chapter 7 under "Designing a Zoan Devil Fruit Sheet" in the One Piece Dungeons and Devil Fruits PHB.

    Hybrid Form. You can use your action to enter a "hybrid" zoan state, combining a mix of qualities from both your humanoid form and beast form together for a temporary period of time. You follow the rules given in Chapter 7 under "Designing a Zoan Devil Fruit Sheet" in the One Piece Dungeons and Devil Fruits PHB.

    Awakening. Upon the awakening of your Zoan Devil Fruit power, when you enter your Hybrid Form, you can temporarily enter your Awakened State, which lasts for 1 minute.

    While your Awakened State is active, your hit point maximum and hit points increase by 50, your weapon attacks and unarmed strike attacks deal extra damage of their primary damage type equal to your character level, and you are able to select an additional hybrid form option. Furthermore, at the start of each of your turns for the duration of this state, you regain hit points equivalent to your character level + your Constitution modifier.

    Should the duration of your Awakened State expire, you hold the option to extend its span for an additional minute, at the cost of incurring a level of exhaustion. If needed, you can further extend this state by enduring an extra level of exhaustion for each additional minute. These levels of exhaustion can only be removed by completing a long rest.

    Once your Awakened State ends, it can't be activated again for another 24 hours.

    CHAPTER 3 | VERY RARE ZOAN

    Ryu Ryu no Mi, Model: Stegosaurus

    Devil Fruit, Very Rare

    Description. This zoan devil fruit allows its user to transform into a stegosaurus.

Furthermore, at the start of each of your turns for the duration of this state, you regain hit points equivalent to your character level + your Constitution modifier.

    Should the duration of your Awakened State expire, you hold the option to extend its span for an additional minute, at the cost of incurring a level of exhaustion. If needed, you can further extend this state by enduring an extra level of exhaustion for each additional minute. These levels of exhaustion can only be removed by completing a long rest.

    Once your Awakened State ends, it can't be activated again for another 24 hours.

    Ryu Ryu no Mi, Model: Ankylosaurus

    Devil Fruit, Very Rare

    Type. Ancient Zoan

    Fruit appearance. This devil fruit appears as a rough orange mango with short rugged spikes across its surface and a hard bulbous stem.

    Description. This zoan devil fruit allows its user to transform into an ankylosaurus.

    Sea Weakness. You are weak to water and seastone.

    Beast Shape. As an action, you are able to transform into an Ankylosaurus from the standard 5th Edition Monster Manual. You follow the rules given in Chapter 7 under "Designing a Zoan Devil Fruit Sheet" in the One Piece Dungeons and Devil Fruits PHB.

    Hybrid Form. You can use your action to enter a "hybrid" zoan state, combining a mix of qualities from both your humanoid form and beast form together for a temporary period of time. You follow the rules given in Chapter 7 under "Designing a Zoan Devil Fruit Sheet" in the One Piece Dungeons and Devil Fruits PHB.

    Awakening. Upon the awakening of your Zoan Devil Fruit power, when you enter your Hybrid Form, you can temporarily enter your Awakened State, which lasts for 1 minute.

    While your Awakened State is active, your hit point maximum and hit points increase by 50, your weapon attacks and unarmed strike attacks deal extra damage of their primary damage type equal to your character level, and you are able to select an additional hybrid form option. Furthermore, at the start of each of your turns for the duration of this state, you regain hit points equivalent to your character level + your Constitution modifier.

    Should the duration of your Awakened State expire, you hold the option to extend its span for an additional minute, at the cost of incurring a level of exhaustion. If needed, you can further extend this state by enduring an extra level of exhaustion for each additional minute. These levels of exhaustion can only be removed by completing a long rest.

    Once your Awakened State ends, it can't be activated again for another 24 hours.

    Description. This zoan devil fruit allows its user to transform into a tyrannosaurus rex.

    Sea Weakness. You are weak to water and seastone.
